Without question this qualifies as a unisex scent, anyone can get away with wearing this. <br />
<br />

To me it is a woody, Vanilla and chestnut fragrance, very well balanced. Linear, yes. Very comforting, not cloying. Perfect from mid September to February in western Europe.<br />
She hasn't a huge sillage but she stays on clothes and skin , a bit less. Put some on your scarf as well for instant bliss and confort putting your nose into it during the day !</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2317335"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2317335#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2317271" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1868704">sharpteethstarlet</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-14">10/14/24 20:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I was so sure I was gonna like this one, that I bought a decant instead of a sample. The aesthetic, the main accord’s palette and the situation it wants to recreate are so right up my alley.<br />
<br />
Unfortunately, there is a specific note that I find really disturbing. Similarly to some other iteration of that same note in other perfumes - like Frustration and, the worst offender, Fat Electrician by ELDO - the way this fragrance tries to interpret the chestnut smells very synthetic, to the point it even makes me slightly nauseous. <br />
It’s a shame because it’s a delicious smell in real life, and an interesting one to recreate in a perfume, except I didn’t manage to find a good, realistic interpretation of it that doesn’t have this weird artificial undertone.<br />
<br />
The warm woods in the background that start coming up after an hour or so finally seem to hint to the cozy-christmasy scenery I was hoping for: I wish it was just those and a good smokiness I personally don’t perceive here. Instead, I had to wash my wrists to make that “plastic chestnut” scent less powerful because it was making me feel sick.<br />
<br />
(@sharpteethstarlet on TT for more reviews 🌝)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2315972"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2315972#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2315951" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This can be layered with some chocolaty scents, will try like that</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2310189"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2310189#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2309514" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2305253" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Taya_77"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2174317"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2174317.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Taya_77" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2305253ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2305253" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2174317">Taya_77</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-04">10/04/24 19:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I love everything about this! Out of all the fragrances I've tried the past few months, BTF is my favorite. It's so incredibly warm and cozy and comforting. I don't agree it smells like your clothes after a bonfire. That smell is very harsh and bitter, pungent almost, I actually hate it. While this obviously does smell like burning wood, there's nothing bitter or pungent about it, it's SWEET and delectable. It evokes a charred hunk of fragrant wood, smoking amongst the red glowing embers of a dying fire. Chestnuts are roasting on the fire too. And then come the roasted marshmallows, partly charred, partly melting all gooey onto the embers.<br />
<br />
I don't get the orange blossom, I'm not sure where that factors in. But this blend is just perfect. It doesn't scream Christmas necessarily, but fall and winter. It's not versatile. It doesn't really smell like a perfume... it smells like what it is. It ALMOST should be a candle instead, but never crosses that line for me; I find this very wearable. And completely unisex although it does kinda make me imagine a burly lumberjack coming in from the snow to stoke the fire in his mountain cabin.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I love it. However, I am conflicted on whether or not I love it on me. Fragrances turn particularly sweet on my skin, and that is especially true of fragrances that are actually sweet in the first place, such as this. I have also only ever smelled it on women where I live, which makes it all that more difficult for me to "get away with" culturally. I think I am going to purchase a bottle soon anyway though. I tried this while I was on a vacation with my family and they were blown away by the fragrance and how well it evoked the image and idea expressed by its name while making it a legitimate and wearable fragrance (rather than something you would associate with a scented candle). <br />
Humorously, despite my mom having an absolute hatred for sweet fragrances on men, to the extent that she finds even Bleu de Chanel Parfum and Chanel Allure Homme Sport Superleggera to smell like "perfume" on my skin (I don't agree), she actually thinks it smells smokey and masculine. I would say that it absolutely, without a doubt, that it is built as a unisex fragrance. However, I believe your skin chemistry and cultural environment will play significant roles in whether or not it works for you. One I make an actual purchase I will come back and give it a full and legitimate review. For now, these are just my thoughts.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2304669"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2304669#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2304624" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; 1: One can't not judge a perfume by the top notes and decide "it's not for me"; "it's too cloying"; etc. Always wait for the dry down.<br />

align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2289735"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2289735#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2289508" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2289508" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="EvanGiorgioArmani"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2258882"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2258882.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="EvanGiorgioArmani" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2289508ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2289508" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2258882">EvanGiorgioArmani</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-20">09/20/24 12:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Gosh...where do I start. This fragrance is so underrated in my opinion. Like some others have said, this fragrance was my very first that I bought and it began my fragrance journey and hobby during covid in 2019. I have loved it ever since I first smelled it. Keep in mind, this was before I ever smelled a fragrance, so my nose at that time was very new...and still I loved it. As a man in my mid-20s, my thoughts of it remain the same as I still fall in love with it over and over again. Now that I have firmly entered the niche world of fragrance, By The Fireplace could honestly be sold by a niche brand and it would be a great seller. For example, if Xerjoff bottled this and sold it as a fireplace-type of scent, it would be a popular choice in their portfolio. I recommend sampling first, as it is definitely a complex scent and you may not vibe with it. Like myself, I sampled first and it blew me away, and I am happy that it did because it is a significant member of my fragrance wardrobe alongside my niche. <br />
<br />
By The Fireplace, to me, smells niche. Is it the best ever blended scent? Absolutely not. But I am addicted to that iconic smoky, boozy, sweet, nutty, and sexy aura. By The Fireplace puts me in a certain mood similar to Haltane by PDM or Starlight by Xerjoff, and that mood is feeling utterly calm and content while smelling sexy, warm, and cozy. Honestly, I think I might reach for those two fragrances more so than this, just because those pack a heavier punch and are simply higher quality than this. It is not quite versatile, but who cares. It is such a great fragrance! Performance is good, not great - around 7 hours for me. As a typical edt, this fragrance projects heavily in the first two hours, then it becomes a comfortable skin scent for the remainder of its lasting time. Wish it lasted longer though. This fragrance will always stay with me and will carry symbolic meaning to me. That is, THE fragrance that started my journey in the art of perfumery. It is my love and joy! <br />
<br />
8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2289508"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2289508#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2288870" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2288870" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Leoambard"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1948149"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1948149.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Leoambard" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2288870ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2288870" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1948149">Leoambard</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-19">09/19/24 22:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've owned By the Fireplace for five years now, and it is one of my favorites of all time. It was also the first perfume I purchased, and it kicked off my interest in perfumery. I live in a cold and rainy part of the world, so I wear this nine out of twelve months of the year. The main notes are sweet vanilla with a lot of smoke reminiscent of a campfire. I get a little bit of warm spiciness and caramelized orange, but they are quite subtle and fade quickly as the scent dries down. By the Fireplace lasts 12+ hours on my skin easily and lasts for multiple days on my clothes. The one issue with this perfume is that it is not great for layering; the smokiness is just too strong. <br />
<br />
Smell: 10/10<br />
Longevity: 9.5/10<br />
Versatility: 8/10<br />
Uniqueness: 6.5/10<br />
Value: 7/10<br />
Layering compatibility: 5<br />
Overall: 7.7</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2288870"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2288870#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2288420" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Well, it feels like that. The skin touching a smell. I figured you can, because scent is made of molecules and i sometimes forget that. To touch this fragrance makes me excited ( not in the hormonal way, for at least 20 seconds) and i want to touch it more due to how exciting it is to do it. Its the feeling of touching a cloud. Not in the sensational way, but to put the excitement in a way that others could feel, if not, imagine. The scent itself is quite eepy deepy. I feel as though a warm sweater of felt is touching my shoulders, something to be excited about(this time in the hormonal, excruciatingly happy way). Its unusual to feel such a thing in the minds of others, but objects just please me, and i prefer the touch of it to that of a human. Filthy human hands which feel emotion and show touch only when they feel a need to, can only use their brains, nothing more. Fragrances dont do that though. They have no self control. They linger around you for as long as they want. Which is why in some cases, they can be polarizing. But i like it, because they dont care if you get a headache whoopy woop. This fellow bottle is something id like inside of me. That cant be gay though, because its an object, not a fellow dingleberry owner with some STD. "my little baby boy", as Me &amp; my would put it. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1962169">emilybecca</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-11">09/11/24 11:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When I spray this I instantly think not just of winter, sitting by the fire, but also some summer &amp; fall nights cozied up at bonfires and campfires. <br />
<br />
I love By the Fireplace. Amongst the perfumes found at Sephora, this is unique and intriguing. The smokiness is photorealistic to my nose, but I never feel it in the back of my throat (like I do with Commodity Milk Expressive). About a half hour after application, this settles into a subtly sweet, ever-so-slightly smoky, PERFECT vanilla scent. The drydown is worth it. In winter I often apply this at night, feel cozy smelling the opening, then let it dry down while I sleep and wake up smelling like heaven!<br />
<br />
One of my favorites. This lasts a long time on my skin, about 8-10 hours.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2279278"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2279278#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2279174" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2276462" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="beesbuzzing"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2242731"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="beesbuzzing" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2276462ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2276462" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2242731">beesbuzzing</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-08">09/08/24 22:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It smells like an active burning fire, with grey smoke rising in the air mixed with a sweet chestnut scent. This fragrance is amazing for cold days, as the harsh ash cuts through cold air, and the hint of sweetness adds a softness to it. <br />
<br />
This is my snowy day fragrance, and I swear it smells better in cold dry weather. <br />
<br />
The best way to describe this fragrance is to compare it to when you are walking outside on a freezing fall day and you suddenly get a whiff of ash. It's even comparable to when you are walking outside very late at night and get a whiff of distant wood smoke mixed with the sweet perfume you are already wearing.<br />
<br />
It's quite nice and very confronting (ash/smoke smells are very confronting in general), and lasts quite well for an EDT. My advice is to spray this on top of rich body oil to help with its longevity. <br />
<br />
The only thing is that (it may just be my skin) but sometimes it dries down very sweet, and other days it dries down like a cool powder. Either way, the whiffs I get throughout the day are very confronting and cozy. This smell does not work well in hot or humid weather, so if you want to properly enjoy the scent, try it on a very cold dry day - it makes all the difference. <br />
<br />
An interesting idea by Replica to imitate a burning fire, makes me want to find more fragrances that mimic a fire now.<br />
<br />
9/10 for having the idea itself</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2276462"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2276462#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276365" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This scent immediately transports you to memories of roasting marshmallows around a fire, and the smokiness calms down to reveal a sweet, caramelised vanilla scent.<br />
The longevity is somewhat better than other scents by MM due to its bold notes but the dry down becomes a bit difficult to smell after a short while. However, it's a nice progression from a loud smoky scent to an intimate sugary smell, which is beautiful. Slightly too heavy for warm weather, but perfect for autumn and winter, curled up with a cup of coffee in your favourite blanket, or walking in the autumn breeze.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; While the rest of the collection didn’t intrigue me as much, this one stood out, especially since I love vanilla and smoky scents. Finally, I ordered a 10 ml decant, and even before spraying it, I could smell the gorgeousness.<br />
<br />
This perfume truly evokes the warmth of a fireplace, but the smokiness is more complex. It’s very smoky, but there’s an underlying creamy, woody sweetness that balances it beautifully. It’s what I imagine a “cool” person would smell like. While I quit smoking after college, this scent has an authentic smokiness that reminds me of that vibe, which I think is pretty cool for a perfume to pull off.<br />
<br />
The scent is comforting and nostalgic, taking me back to bonfires and carefree times spent with friends. It definitely lived up to my expectations, and I’m planning to buy a full bottle. I’ll also be checking out other scents from the Replica line, like Jazz Club.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2276175"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2276175#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276165" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2276165" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="feathering"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2153375"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="feathering" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2276165ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2276165" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2153375">feathering</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-08">09/08/24 14:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When I initially smelled By The Fireplace in Sephora, I was both in love with this scent and new to perfume. So I bought a full size secondhand, and made it through roughly 1/5 of the bottle before I came to the delayed epiphany that I don't think I actually like gourmands.<br />
<br />
From afar, in passing, I can see how this is well-loved. Even for me, it was love at first scent, but as time went on, the vividly sweet marshmallow became way too cloying for me. The smoky woodiness had lost it's punch, and all I could focus on was how confrontational and upstaging the vanilla had become. There was no crispness on my skin, no bite from the cloves, pink pepper, or juniper. Only round, warm, and soft. Of course, this is the pleasure of trial and error, and also a lesson for me on impulse. <br />
<br />
That said, this is an alluring scent that's popular for a reason. It either just didn't cooperate with my skin chemistry, or I'm not built to be a gourmand-wearer. I wouldn't even be bold enough to say I dislike it, but the admittedly impressive projection and longevity meant I was stuck wading through a very dominant cloud of saccharine vanilla all day. I can certainly appreciate it momentarily, though, and might even appreciate it more on someone else. It just didn't belong in my personal collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2276165"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2276165#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2275566" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Today I finally got to smell it and oh boy, was I not expecting the smell. The opening is not that great and the first 5 to 15 mins are incredibly awful. It might just be how it mixes with my skin but it just smelt like my skin was burnt with a teeny touch of sweetness. Now after it's dried down for maybe half an hour to an hour, it definitely smell better. I do like this smell, but having to deal with that awful smell for the first hour, no thanks. The dupe also doens't have a great opening but mainly because its overly sweet. However, it smells better after it dries down in 10 minutes or so and it smells close enough, and in my opinion, nicer.<br />
I wouldn't buy by the fireplace. If i got it gifted I would love to say I'd use it because I can enjoy the smell but I don't know if its good enough to have to deal with the first awful hour.<br />
<br />
opening: 1/10<br />
after drydown: 6/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2270099"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2270099#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2269174" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I was really enticed by the notes- woody and smoky scents are among my faves and a pink pepper opening is always great, but this one just smells like a chestnut bomb to me. Lots of vanilla (of dubious quality), lots of chestnut, and some smoke. It has a really similar to scent DNA to Whispers in the Library which I really couldn't stand either, so if that one bothers you, By the Fireplace won't be your thing. It reminds me of a particularly noxious chestnut-forward perfume that a regular substitute teacher wore at my elementary school- I could always tell when she was subbing the second I stepped foot inside the school (went to quite a large school, she stunk up the whole building).<br />
This one's no comparison to Jazz Club- it's popular for a reason. You don't want to smell LIKE the fireplace and marshmallows, you want to smell amazing BY the fireplace.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2268310"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2268310#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2266527" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1951661">Heliotrope72</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-30">08/30/24 01:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>MBTI: INFJ, INFP<br />
Who is she: 🏕️ An Elden ring checkpoint fire. You're safe here. <br />
<br />
Vanilla with a woody smoke twist. Unconventional, but comforting. Projects a lot.<br />
It's like drinking a vanilla cappucino in your green backyard on a late summer / autumn night, while the kids are running a campfire and toasting marshmallows next door. <br />
<br />
I'd personally say that the sweet burnt guaiac wood is the predominant scent, followed by the interchaging bite of smoke and sugary vanillic sweetness. <br />
It really does mimic burnt sugar in a smokehouse, but somehow it's done elegantly enough to wear in casual settings.<br />
<br />
It's an evening scent for me, I tend to put it on indoors while I work on my laptop at night, trying to make sense of personal projects. <br />
It works as a day scent if the place where you work or live is pretty cold and sterile. <br />
<br />
If I had any complaints, I'd say that the scent is a bit screechy - as it definetly could've been better blended. <br />
I would personally love if Guerlain or Amouage made a scent of this profile, but knowing my luck I imagine they'd chuck in musk or iris here, <br />
which is - frankly - totally uneccessary. I wish the vanilla was better quality. <br />
<br />
Otherwise, the execution is good as is, albeit a tad linear.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2265545"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2265545#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2265516" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I am going to let this macerate for a few months, then I will report back</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2261458"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2261458#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2261086" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2231229">Ophiuchus135</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-25">08/25/24 21:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>In settings where I need a fragrance to last a long time and make a clear statement, this one's the way to go. The smokiness and marshmallowy-spicy sweetness is strong, and it fares very well on nights out in crowded settings. It finds its place in lively social gatherings at night and bonfires (the name really does it justice). I find myself needing to apply it sparingly, as the sweetness can be almost cloying, and over-spraying brings out an almost burnt savoriness, like marinated meat that caramelized on a grill for too long. I'll still smell it on my jackets days after.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2261086"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2261086#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2260993" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2227701">jackawad</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-25">08/25/24 19:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So I originally walked into David Jones wanting to try out Jazz Club as it receives way more hype than this on social media. But when I noticed By the Fireplace, I decided to try out both on my skin and said I'd come back later. I'll admit, this fragrance opens up harshly with smoky wood and may easily offend others if you overspray it. However, once I smelled the dry down of both, I made my decision right there on the spot. The dry down of By the Fireplace is honestly what saves it, and I wouldn't even think about spending AUD 235 for a bottle of it if the dry down wasn't as good. This is a woody, smoky and sweeter fragrance than Jazz Club and is unisex. I bought a bottle and I think its great to wear on nights out in the winter. It reminds me of the sensual vibe I get from a fragrance like SWY Intensely but much more smoky and less juvenile. Great fragrance, but maybe not worth the price tag if you're not into it. 9.2/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2260993"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2260993#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2260388" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; *Fall/Winter<br />
*5 ⭐️<br />
<br />
One thing you can count on with the Replica line is the scent is literally the name with the main notes listed on the label. By the Fireplace is a smoky (think the smoke of a fireplace or bonfire), with a sweetness (think marshmallows being roasted over said bonfire),  and a hint of toasted chestnuts. This was a love at first sniff for me. It got even better in the dry down.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2244238"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2244238#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2243779" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If you take a look at the main accords pyramid here on fragrantica you would appreciate my point. All three are warm scents to say the least and very balsamic and resinous which makes all of them very aromatic. Each scent then uses other complimenting woods and nuts to give it more depth/intensity and a hint of a particular herb or spice. Each again has its own characteristic sweetness. While autumn vibes appears to me to be the more sweet of the three, myrrh and tonka has the very noticeable lavender whereas by the fireplace's smokiness is it's best selling point. Of the three JM Myrrh and tonka outmatched the Maison Margiela two in terms of longevity. These scents would be beautiful to wear during the coldest days. In heat and humidity these would be cloying.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2243779"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2243779#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2242950" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's a date night fragrance.  If you are not in a relationship or dating, then there is not point in wearing it as your signature.  That's just my take though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2238511"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2238511#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2236881" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2236881"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2236881#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2234147" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2234147" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ryanfarthill"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2208404"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2208404.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ryanfarthill" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2234147ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2234147" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2208404">ryanfarthill</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-30">07/30/24 17:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>In the heart of Paris, on a cobblestone street lined with quaint boutiques, there was a small, enchanting perfume shop called "L’Essence du Temps." The shop was renowned not just for its exquisite collection of fragrances but also for the stories that accompanied each scent. Among the many bottles that lined the shelves, one stood out: "By the Fireplace."<br />
<br />
This fragrance was more than just a scent; it was an olfactory journey into the heart of a story. The tale began in a centuries-old manor house nestled in the French countryside. The manor was surrounded by sprawling oak trees and rolling meadows, and at its center was a grand fireplace that had witnessed countless gatherings over the years.<br />
<br />
The fireplace was the heart of the manor, a place where stories were shared and memories were made. It was here that the matriarch of the family, a woman named Geneviève, would gather her loved ones every winter. She had a penchant for creating an atmosphere of warmth and comfort, and it was her ritual to blend essential oils and spices into a unique scent that filled the manor during these gatherings. This blend of aromatic woods, smoky embers, and subtle hints of vanilla became synonymous with the feeling of home and coziness.<br />
<br />
One particularly snowy winter, Geneviève’s granddaughter, Isabelle, returned from her studies in Paris. The visit was meant to be a brief respite from the bustling city life, a chance to reconnect with her roots. Isabelle had always been enchanted by her grandmother's ability to create such a magical ambiance. She spent hours by the fireplace, savoring the blend of aromas that danced through the air.<br />
<br />
One evening, as the snowflakes fell softly outside, Isabelle asked her grandmother about the secret behind the scent that made the manor feel so inviting. Geneviève smiled, her eyes twinkling like the firelight. She revealed that the scent was not just a blend of ingredients but a manifestation of the memories and emotions that had accumulated over time.<br />
<br />
Inspired, Isabelle decided to capture the essence of the fireplace and the memories it held. With her grandmother’s guidance, she carefully recorded the ingredients and the proportions used to create the fragrance. The blend was a complex symphony: the smoky warmth of birchwood, the crisp freshness of winter air, the creamy sweetness of vanilla, and the subtle spice of clove and cinnamon.<br />
<br />
Upon returning to Paris, Isabelle collaborated with a renowned perfumer to bring the scent to life in a bottle. After months of crafting and refining, "By the Fireplace" was born. The fragrance was a tribute to the comforting embrace of home, the shared moments of joy, and the rich tapestry of family history.<br />
<br />
When "By the Fireplace" was introduced at L’Essence du Temps, it quickly became a sensation. Each spritz was a momentary escape to the warmth and comfort of a distant, cherished place. The scent evoked the sensation of sitting by a roaring fire, wrapped in a soft blanket, surrounded by loved ones and laughter.<br />
<br />
Customers from around the world were enchanted by the story that accompanied the fragrance. For many, it became a way to recreate a sense of warmth and nostalgia in their own lives. Whether they were in a bustling city apartment or a quiet countryside home, "By the Fireplace" offered a moment of solace and connection to something deeply comforting and universal.<br />
<br />
And so, in a small shop on a cobblestone street in Paris, the story of a beloved fireplace lived on through each bottle of "By the Fireplace," inviting everyone who experienced it to find their own piece of home and warmth in the scent of a bygone era.<br />
<br />

In my view it leans more feminine but that may be the way it dries down on my skin which is very vanilla, nutty, cashmere. It's strength is the nostalgia and almost protective warmth it elicits. I can't smell smoke like others can it just smells very woody- more snug log cabin than straight up fireplace. <br />
I live in a country without seasons so honestly wear this year round. It's more of an evening scent but I don't think it's just for cooler weather especially if you layer which I think this scent is perfect for as it gives a really nice vanilla woody base. E.g. Layered with Maison Margiela replica Beach Walk and it's giving a sparkling late summer evening sat by a camp fire on the beach. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2219546" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="UNATCO"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2136373"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2136373.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="UNATCO" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2219546ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2219546" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2136373">UNATCO</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-15">07/15/24 16:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>By the Fireplace opens with a pleasant smoky, woody accord. It's the kind of scent that you smell after a few logs are smouldering from the other side of the room. While that smoke may fade into the background somewhat quickly the wood note stays and a nutty, sweet smell emerges. The chestnut and vanilla mix together to create a warm accord that reminds my nose of freshly baked desserts around the holidays.<br />
<br />
This fragrance paints a vivid image in my mind of a time towards the end of the year when theres a chill in the air, the days are getting shorter and you long to be around the people you love. That comforting aroma of being home is exactly what you get with this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2219546"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2219546#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2218821" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1820254">dfreeman</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-11">07/11/24 22:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Oh By the Fireplace, where do I begin. Love at first sniff and the same reaction came from my partner at the time. Memories of comfort and love have became intertwined with this scent. By the Fireplace will always hold a dear place in my heart. It's moments like these where one truly understands the beauty of perfumery.<br />
<br />
Personal expierence aside, this is a very intimate perfume. Some may complain about the longevity/projection but I believe this scent would become something it's not if it were to be a beast mode scent; the subtleness of this fragrance is key. <br />
<br />
Simply put, the perfumer had a clear goal for this scent and executed it beautifully.<br />
<br />
10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2215980"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2215980#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2215756" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I think this is the first time I voted "hate" on a scent. I mean, it smells exactly like its name and I would have never picked this up if it wasn't in the sample box but this is way too realistic. It’s not an unpleasant smell per se…but I would NEVER choose to smell like this again. After a few hours of wear, the vanilla finally starts coming through and it actually smells really beautiful, but at that point it just smells like Phlur Vanilla Skin. It has moderate sillage and lasts all day. In terms of perfumes listed as similar—<br />
✔️❌ BBW Vanilla Romance: similar but less smoky and the vanilla isn’t as rich<br />
✔️❌ Champagne Socialist Bonfire Night: similar at first but the smokiness is sharper and more artificial, and the vanilla doesn’t come through as strongly<br />
✔️❌ Urban Outfitters Crème Caramel: similarly smoky but the vanilla isn’t nearly as rich as it wears<br />
❌✔️ Zara Supreme Vanilla: not similar until the smokiness of By The Fireplace wears off<br />
❌ Commodity Milk: a lightly woody and grassy scent<br />
❌ Navitus Mahni Cassonade: much sweeter and nowhere near as smoky<br />
❌ YSL Babycat: more peppery and intense</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="2194268"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=2194268#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2194176" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;                             <div id="parent1327443" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1327443" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="heatherrose"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1312562"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1312562.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="heatherrose" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1327443ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1327443" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1312562">heatherrose</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-04-17">04/17/21 22:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It is so innately human to have a connection with fire and burning wood. This is a fragrance that will truly transport you and ground you in the memories you have with fire. We all have this connection - this memory of sitting By the Fireplace. It's warm, sweet burning wood, sticky marshmallows, cloves, smoke and vanilla. It's so delicious. <br />
<br />
On a more personal note, this fragrance has helped me mend my relationship with fire after having lost my home in the California wildfires this past year. It truly is something special and a fragrance I admire and adore.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="1327443"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=1327443#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1085298" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Immediately I am transported to late autumn and the smell of bonfires, the crunch of leaves and the sight of my breath like smoke in the air.<br />

It will smell wonderful from late October through to Christmas.  As much as I'm enjoying this surprisingly lovely late summer weather in the UK I'm looking forward to lighting my fire in a few months' time and snuggling up with this fragrance on.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc639738" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="spcmiller"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/144691"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.144691.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="spcmiller" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Oud-Wood-Parfum-89988.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.89988.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Oud Wood Parfum"title="Oud Wood Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma639738ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck8x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd639738" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/144691">spcmiller</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-10-17">10/17/15 12:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Here is the note breakdown:<br />
<br />
Top Notes:  Pink pepper, Orange flower petals, Clove oil<br />
<br />
Heart Notes: Chestnut accord, Gaïac wood oil, Cade oil  <br />
<br />
Base Notes: Vanilla accord, Peru balsam, Cashmeran<br />
<br />
I just received a decant of this stuff and it's not as great at the others they have produced.  Initially, I get a very cedary/piney opening with a bitter smokiness to it, with a slight amount of sweetness in there for good measure. I get a resinous background that's an almost pine-like smell as the scent progresses.  I don't know that I would be able to detect the chestnut accord if my life depended on it. <br />
<br />
As it dries down, the bitterness subsides and a vanilla semi-sweetness emerges, but the woody smokiness never goes entirely away.<br />
<br />
We used to have a wood stove to warm our house in the wintertime and this smells pretty close to that to include the bitterness of the pinewood smoke.  It smells like my father used to smell after he stoked the fire; he would smell like this for 30 or so minutes afterwards.<br />
<br />
Personally, this is a 'pass'.  I LOVE MMM, but this is just a bit too authentic for me.  I can't imagine a situation where I would want to intentionally smell like burnt wood...summer or winter.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="639738"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=639738#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1686220" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1072408" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="cocofluff"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1141155"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1141155.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="cocofluff" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Etat-Libre-d-Orange/Bendelirious-4511.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.4511.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Bendelirious"title="Bendelirious"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1072408ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1072408" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1141155">cocofluff</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-06-22">06/22/19 21:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>What in the realistic fireplace is going on here? I don't know how they did it but MM made such a realistic perfume. It smells just like I'm sitting by a stone fireplace and roasting chestnuts. This is an amazing fragrance. I totally respect it! The only thing I don't enjoy is the cashmeran note. <br />
-</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="1072408"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=1072408#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent881399" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc881399" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Minnie02"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1041618"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1041618.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Minnie02" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma881399ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd881399" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1041618">Minnie02</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-11-17">11/17/17 18:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This scent really wowed me at first spray. Originally, I didn't even want to test it, why would you want to smell like a fireplace? And the Peru balsam was concerning as I'm not a fan of it. Out of curiosity, I sprayed it on paper, and then on my skin. My very first impression is that it truly smells like the sweet and smokey fragrance of pine or cedar wood burning in a fireplace, very pleasant and soothing. However, I still have to wonder why would you want to smell like that - it would be nice for an ambient candle maybe...<br />
<br />
And then after a few minutes, as the top notes start to dissipate, it becomes kind of cloying and nauseating. There is Peru balsam in Michael Kors Midnight Shimmer, which is what I believe made that scent unbearable to me, and unfortunately, as By The Fireplace is drying down, what I believe is the Peru balsam starts showing up and that's where it loses me too. To my nose, the dry down has a medicinal scent mixed with sweet smokiness. Odd combination.<br />
<br />
It's definitely an interesting, intriguing, and different perfume, but it's not my thing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="31623"comment_id="881399"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Maison-Martin-Margiela/By-the-Fireplace-31623.html?ccid=881399#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="31623" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
